(comment "CPSA 3.6.9")
(comment "Extracted shapes")

(herald "Grant Negotiation and Authorization Protocol" (limit 5000)
  (comment
    "This protocol allows a piece of software, the client instance, to request delegated authorization to resource servers and to request direct information"))

(comment "CPSA 3.6.9")

(comment "All input read from GNAP.scm")

(comment "Step count limited to 5000")

(defprotocol gnap_simple basic
  (defrole client
    (vars (c as rs name)
      (access uri c_token acess_token_1 acess_token_2 rights data))
    (trace (send (enc c access (ltk c as)))
      (recv (enc uri c_token (ltk c as)))
      (send (enc c_token (ltk c as)))
      (recv (enc acess_token_1 rights (ltk c as)))
      (send (enc acess_token_1 (ltk c rs)))
      (send (enc acess_token_1 (ltk c as)))
      (recv (enc acess_token_2 (ltk c as)))
      (send (enc acess_token_2 (ltk c rs)))
      (send (enc acess_token_2 (ltk c as)))))
  (defrole authorization_server
    (vars (c as name)
      (access uri c_token acess_token_1 acess_token_2 rights data))
    (trace (recv (enc c access (ltk c as)))
      (send (enc uri c_token (ltk c as)))
      (recv (enc c_token (ltk c as)))
      (send (enc acess_token_1 rights (ltk c as)))
      (recv (enc acess_token_1 (ltk c as)))
      (send (enc acess_token_2 (ltk c as)))
      (recv (enc acess_token_2 (ltk c as)))))
  (defrole resource_server
    (vars (c rs name) (acess_token_1 acess_token_2 data))
    (trace (recv (enc acess_token_1 (ltk c rs)))
      (recv (enc acess_token_2 (ltk c rs))))))

(defskeleton gnap_simple
  (vars (access uri c_token acess_token_1 acess_token_2 rights data)
    (c as rs name))
  (defstrand client 9 (access access) (uri uri) (c_token c_token)
    (acess_token_1 acess_token_1) (acess_token_2 acess_token_2)
    (rights rights) (c c) (as as) (rs rs))
  (non-orig (ltk c as) (ltk c rs))
  (comment "")
  (traces
    ((send (enc c access (ltk c as)))
      (recv (enc uri c_token (ltk c as)))
      (send (enc c_token (ltk c as)))
      (recv (enc acess_token_1 rights (ltk c as)))
      (send (enc acess_token_1 (ltk c rs)))
      (send (enc acess_token_1 (ltk c as)))
      (recv (enc acess_token_2 (ltk c as)))
      (send (enc acess_token_2 (ltk c rs)))
      (send (enc acess_token_2 (ltk c as)))))
  (label 0)
  (unrealized (0 1) (0 3) (0 6))
  (origs)
  (comment "2 in cohort - 2 not yet seen"))

(defskeleton gnap_simple
  (vars
    (access uri c_token acess_token_2 access-0 uri-0 c_token-0
      acess_token_1 rights data) (c as rs as-0 name))
  (defstrand client 9 (access access) (uri uri) (c_token c_token)
    (acess_token_1 uri) (acess_token_2 acess_token_2) (rights c_token)
    (c c) (as as) (rs rs))
  (defstrand authorization_server 2 (access access) (uri uri)
    (c_token c_token) (c c) (as as))
  (defstrand client 8 (access access-0) (uri uri-0) (c_token c_token-0)
    (acess_token_1 acess_token_1) (acess_token_2 acess_token_2)
    (rights rights) (c c) (as as-0) (rs as))
  (precedes ((0 0) (1 0)) ((1 1) (0 1)) ((2 7) (0 6)))
  (non-orig (ltk c as) (ltk c rs))
  (operation encryption-test (added-strand client 8)
    (enc acess_token_2 (ltk c as)) (0 6))
  (traces
    ((send (enc c access (ltk c as)))
      (recv (enc uri c_token (ltk c as)))
      (send (enc c_token (ltk c as)))
      (recv (enc uri c_token (ltk c as))) (send (enc uri (ltk c rs)))
      (send (enc uri (ltk c as))) (recv (enc acess_token_2 (ltk c as)))
      (send (enc acess_token_2 (ltk c rs)))
      (send (enc acess_token_2 (ltk c as))))
    ((recv (enc c access (ltk c as)))
      (send (enc uri c_token (ltk c as))))
    ((send (enc c access-0 (ltk c as-0)))
      (recv (enc uri-0 c_token-0 (ltk c as-0)))
      (send (enc c_token-0 (ltk c as-0)))
      (recv (enc acess_token_1 rights (ltk c as-0)))
      (send (enc acess_token_1 (ltk c as)))
      (send (enc acess_token_1 (ltk c as-0)))
      (recv (enc acess_token_2 (ltk c as-0)))
      (send (enc acess_token_2 (ltk c as)))))
  (label 82)
  (parent 0)
  (unrealized)
  (shape)
  (maps
    ((0)
      ((c c) (as as) (rs rs) (access access) (uri uri) (c_token c_token)
        (acess_token_1 uri) (acess_token_2 acess_token_2)
        (rights c_token))))
  (origs))
